### Query
like this:
def main():
    # initialize chat history once per session
    if "chat_history" not in st.session_state:
        st.session_state.chat_history = []  # list of {"role": "user"/"assistant", "content": str}


    ensure_dir(PDF_DIR)
    ensure_dir(DB_DIR)


    # ✅ Test embedding model dimension (runs once at startup)
    embeddings = HuggingFaceEmbeddings(
        model_name=EMBED_MODEL,
        model_kwargs={"device": "cpu"}
    )
    test_vec = embeddings.embed_query("test")
    logger.info(f"✅ Embedding model: {EMBED_MODEL}, dimension: {len(test_vec)}")


    
    st.set_page_config(page_title="Respiratory AI Assistant", layout="wide")


    st.markdown(
        '<h1 style="text-align:center;color:#2E86AB;">🩺 Respiratory AI Assistant</h1>',
        unsafe_allow_html=True,
    )


    with st.sidebar:
        st.header("📊 Database Management")


        status_placeholder = st.empty()
        progress_bar = st.progress(0)


        def progress_update(fname, percent_done, remaining_sec):
            eta_str = (
                f"{int(remaining_sec // 60)}m {int(remaining_sec % 60)}s"
                if remaining_sec > 60
                else f"{int(remaining_sec)}s"
            )
            status_placeholder.text(
                f"Processing: {fname} | {percent_done:.1f}% | ETA: {eta_str}"
            )
            progress_bar.progress(int(percent_done))


        if st.button("🔄 Rebuild Database"):
            warnings = build_db(rebuild=True, progress_callback=progress_update)
            progress_bar.empty()
            status_placeholder.success("Database rebuilt successfully!")
            if warnings:
                with st.expander("⚠️ Build Warnings"):
                    for w in warnings:
                        st.warning(w)


        if st.button("📝 Update Database"):
            warnings = build_db(rebuild=False, progress_callback=progress_update)
            progress_bar.empty()
            status_placeholder.success("Database updated successfully!")
            if warnings:
                with st.expander("⚠️ Update Warnings"):
                    for w in warnings:
                        st.warning(w)


        st.markdown("---")
        st.markdown(
            "• Place PDF files in the `pdfs` folder\n"
            "• Rebuild DB when adding new documents\n"
            "• Update DB for incremental changes"
        )


    # Ensure database exists
    if not os.path.exists(DB_DIR) or not os.listdir(DB_DIR):
        st.error("Database missing! Please add PDFs and build the database in the sidebar.")
        return


    # Show recent conversation
    if "chat_history" in st.session_state and st.session_state.chat_history:
        st.markdown("### 🧵 Conversation so far")
        for turn in st.session_state.chat_history[-8:]:
            role = "You" if turn["role"] == "user" else "Assistant"
            st.markdown(f"**{role}:** {turn['content']}")


    # Question input centered
    st.markdown(
        '<div style="background:#f8f9fa;padding:2rem;border-radius:10px;">',
        unsafe_allow_html=True,
    )
    col1, col2, col3 = st.columns([1, 3, 1])
    with col2:
        st.markdown("### 🤔 Ask Your Respiratory Question")
        query = st.text_area(
            "",
            placeholder="Enter your clinical question here...",
            height=100,
        )
        st.markdown(
            "*Append “\nAnswer without revealing your internal reasoning.” at the end "
            "of the prompt to prevent the model from inventing unsupported details.*"
        )
        search = st.button("🔍 Get Answer")
    st.markdown("</div>", unsafe_allow_html=True)


if query and search:
    # 1) Add user message to history
    st.session_state.chat_history.append({"role": "user", "content": query})


    # 2) Build compact conversation summary (last 6 turns) for the model
    recent_turns = st.session_state.chat_history[-6:]
    chat_context_text = ""
    for turn in recent_turns:
        role = "User" if turn["role"] == "user" else "Assistant"
        chat_context_text += f"{role}: {turn['content']}\n"


    # 3) Retrieval from RAG database
    embeddings = HuggingFaceEmbeddings(
        model_name=EMBED_MODEL,
        model_kwargs={"device": "cpu"},
    )
    store = Chroma(persist_directory=DB_DIR, embedding_function=embeddings)


    retriever = store.as_retriever(
        search_type="mmr",
        search_kwargs={"k": 25, "fetch_k": 60, "lambda_mult": 0.4},
    )
    docs = retriever.invoke(query)


    # DEBUG: inspect retrieved docs
    for i, d in enumerate(docs, 1):
        logger.info(
            f"Doc {i} source={d.metadata.get('source')} "
            f"preview={d.page_content[:400].replace('\n', ' ')}"
        )


    # Limit total context length
    max_chars = 18000
    kb_context = ""
    for d in docs:
        if len(kb_context) + len(d.page_content) > max_chars:
            break
        kb_context += "\n\n" + d.page_content


    # 4) Build prompt with chat history + KB context
    prompt = PromptTemplate(
        template=(
            "You are an expert academic pulmonologist and intensivist.\n"
            "You are chatting with a clinician about a specific case.\n"
            "Use ONLY the information contained in the context AND prior turns of "
            "this chat. If an item is not supported by either, do not invent it.\n\n"
            "Conversation so far:\n{chat_history}\n\n"
            "Retrieved knowledge base context (guidelines, reviews, etc.):\n"
            "{kb_context}\n\n"
            "For the latest user question, if the information is available, "
            "structure the answer into:\n"
            "1. Clinical presentation.\n"
            "2. Investigations (labs, imaging, other tests).\n"
            "3. Diagnosis and differential.\n"
            "4. Management and treatment (including specific medications, "
            "dose ranges, route, and duration when stated in the context).\n"
            "5. Follow‑up, monitoring, and red‑flags.\n\n"
            "Rules:\n"
            "- Respect the ongoing case: if the user asks a follow‑up question "
            "about 'this patient' or 'the previous CT', infer from the chat "
            "history what they refer to.\n"
            "- Every important factual statement must be supported by the "
            "knowledge base context.\n"
            "- Cite each major statement with its source file name "
            "(e.g. \"[source.pdf, pX]\").\n"
            "- If the context does NOT contain enough detail for a point, say so "
            "explicitly rather than guessing.\n"
            "- If the knowledge base overall does not answer the question, reply "
            "exactly: \"Insufficient data in provided materials.\" and nothing more.\n\n"
            "Latest user question:\n{question}\n\n"
            "Answer:\nAnswer without revealing your internal reasoning."
        ),
        input_variables=["chat_history", "kb_context", "question"],
    ).format(
        chat_history=chat_context_text,
        kb_context=kb_context,
        question=query,
    )


    llm = Ollama(model=OLLAMA_MODEL, temperature=0.0, max_tokens=900)
    answer = llm.invoke(prompt)


    # 5) Save assistant answer into chat history
    st.session_state.chat_history.append({"role": "assistant", "content": answer})


    if "[" not in answer:
        st.warning("⚠️ Check sources—some statements may be unsourced.")


    # 6) Nice chat-style rendering (user + assistant bubbles)
    st.markdown("### 🗂️ Recent conversation")
    st.markdown('<div class="chat-container">', unsafe_allow_html=True)


    for msg in st.session_state.chat_history[-10:]:
        role_label = "🧑⚕️ You" if msg["role"] == "user" else "🤖 Assistant"
        bubble_class = "chat-bubble-user" if msg["role"] == "user" else "chat-bubble-assistant"


        st.markdown(
            f"""
            <div class="chat-meta">{role_label}</div>
            <div class="{bubble_class}">{msg["content"]}</div>
            """,
            unsafe_allow_html=True,
        )


    st.markdown("</div>", unsafe_allow_html=True)


    # 7) Sources section under the chat
    st.markdown(
        '<div style="background:#f1f3f4;padding:1rem;border-radius:5px;margin-top:1rem;">',
        unsafe_allow_html=True,
    )
    st.markdown("### 📚 Sources")
    for d in docs:
        st.markdown(f"- {d.metadata['source']}")
    st.markdown("</div>", unsafe_allow_html=True)




    calculator_section()



if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

### Answer
Almost perfect—only two fixes needed: keep if query and search: inside main() and remove the duplicate st.set_page_config inside main() because you already call it at the top.

Here is the corrected structure you can copy‑paste:
def main():
    # initialize chat history once per session
    if "chat_history" not in st.session_state:
        st.session_state.chat_history = []  # list of {"role": "user"/"assistant", "content": str}

    ensure_dir(PDF_DIR)
    ensure_dir(DB_DIR)

    # ✅ Test embedding model dimension (runs once at startup)
    embeddings = HuggingFaceEmbeddings(
        model_name=EMBED_MODEL,
        model_kwargs={"device": "cpu"}
    )
    test_vec = embeddings.embed_query("test")
    logger.info(f"✅ Embedding model: {EMBED_MODEL}, dimension: {len(test_vec)}")

    # (NO st.set_page_config here, you already called it once at top)

    st.markdown(
        '<h1 style="text-align:center;color:#2E86AB;">🩺 Respiratory AI Assistant</h1>',
        unsafe_allow_html=True,
    )

    with st.sidebar:
        ...
        # sidebar code unchanged
        ...

    # Ensure database exists
    if not os.path.exists(DB_DIR) or not os.listdir(DB_DIR):
        st.error("Database missing! Please add PDFs and build the database in the sidebar.")
        return

    # Question input centered
    st.markdown(
        '<div style="background:#f8f9fa;padding:2rem;border-radius:10px;">',
        unsafe_allow_html=True,
    )
    col1, col2, col3 = st.columns([1, 3, 1])
    with col2:
        st.markdown("### 🤔 Ask Your Respiratory Question")
        query = st.text_area(
            "",
            placeholder="Enter your clinical question here...",
            height=100,
        )
        st.markdown(
            "*Append “\nAnswer without revealing your internal reasoning.” at the end "
            "of the prompt to prevent the model from inventing unsupported details.*"
        )
        search = st.button("🔍 Get Answer")
    st.markdown("</div>", unsafe_allow_html=True)

    # >>> this block must be indented inside main() <<<
    if query and search:
        # 1) Add user message to history
        st.session_state.chat_history.append({"role": "user", "content": query})

        # 2) Build compact conversation summary (last 6 turns) for the model
        recent_turns = st.session_state.chat_history[-6:]
        chat_context_text = ""
        for turn in recent_turns:
            role = "User" if turn["role"] == "user" else "Assistant"
            chat_context_text += f"{role}: {turn['content']}\n"

        # 3) Retrieval from RAG database
        embeddings = HuggingFaceEmbeddings(
            model_name=EMBED_MODEL,
            model_kwargs={"device": "cpu"},
        )
        store = Chroma(persist_directory=DB_DIR, embedding_function=embeddings)

        retriever = store.as_retriever(
            search_type="mmr",
            search_kwargs={"k": 25, "fetch_k": 60, "lambda_mult": 0.4},
        )
        docs = retriever.invoke(query)

        # DEBUG: inspect retrieved docs
        for i, d in enumerate(docs, 1):
            logger.info(
                f"Doc {i} source={d.metadata.get('source')} "
                f"preview={d.page_content[:400].replace('\n', ' ')}"
            )

        # Limit total context length
        max_chars = 18000
        kb_context = ""
        for d in docs:
            if len(kb_context) + len(d.page_content) > max_chars:
                break
            kb_context += "\n\n" + d.page_content

        # 4) Build prompt with chat history + KB context
        prompt = PromptTemplate(
            template=(
                "You are an expert academic pulmonologist and intensivist.\n"
                "You are chatting with a clinician about a specific case.\n"
                "Use ONLY the information contained in the context AND prior turns of "
                "this chat. If an item is not supported by either, do not invent it.\n\n"
                "Conversation so far:\n{chat_history}\n\n"
                "Retrieved knowledge base context (guidelines, reviews, etc.):\n"
                "{kb_context}\n\n"
                "For the latest user question, if the information is available, "
                "structure the answer into:\n"
                "1. Clinical presentation.\n"
                "2. Investigations (labs, imaging, other tests).\n"
                "3. Diagnosis and differential.\n"
                "4. Management and treatment (including specific medications, "
                "dose ranges, route, and duration when stated in the context).\n"
                "5. Follow‑up, monitoring, and red‑flags.\n\n"
                "Rules:\n"
                "- Respect the ongoing case: if the user asks a follow‑up question "
                "about 'this patient' or 'the previous CT', infer from the chat "
                "history what they refer to.\n"
                "- Every important factual statement must be supported by the "
                "knowledge base context.\n"
                "- Cite each major statement with its source file name "
                "(e.g. \"[source.pdf, pX]\").\n"
                "- If the context does NOT contain enough detail for a point, say so "
                "explicitly rather than guessing.\n"
                "- If the knowledge base overall does not answer the question, reply "
                "exactly: \"Insufficient data in provided materials.\" and nothing more.\n\n"
                "Latest user question:\n{question}\n\n"
                "Answer:\nAnswer without revealing your internal reasoning."
            ),
            input_variables=["chat_history", "kb_context", "question"],
        ).format(
            chat_history=chat_context_text,
            kb_context=kb_context,
            question=query,
        )

        llm = Ollama(model=OLLAMA_MODEL, temperature=0.0, max_tokens=900)
        answer = llm.invoke(prompt)

        # 5) Save assistant answer into chat history
        st.session_state.chat_history.append({"role": "assistant", "content": answer})

        if "[" not in answer:
            st.warning("⚠️ Check sources—some statements may be unsourced.")

        # 6) Nice chat-style rendering (user + assistant bubbles)
        st.markdown("### 🗂️ Recent conversation")
        st.markdown('<div class="chat-container">', unsafe_allow_html=True)

        for msg in st.session_state.chat_history[-10:]:
            role_label = "🧑⚕️ You" if msg["role"] == "user" else "🤖 Assistant"
            bubble_class = "chat-bubble-user" if msg["role"] == "user" else "chat-bubble-assistant"

            st.markdown(
                f"""
                <div class="chat-meta">{role_label}</div>
                <div class="{bubble_class}">{msg["content"]}</div>
                """,
                unsafe_allow_html=True,
            )

        st.markdown("</div>", unsafe_allow_html=True)

        # 7) Sources section under the chat
        st.markdown(
            '<div style="background:#f1f3f4;padding:1rem;border-radius:5px;margin-top:1rem;">',
            unsafe_allow_html=True,
        )
        st.markdown("### 📚 Sources")
        for d in docs:
            st.markdown(f"- {d.metadata['source']}")
        st.markdown("</div>", unsafe_allow_html=True)

    # calculators at the end
    calculator_section()

Key idea: query only exists inside main(), so if query and search: must be indented under main(), not at the top level.

def ensure_dir(path: str):
    os.makedirs(path, exist_ok=True)


def file_hash(path: str) -> str:
    h = hashlib.md5()
    with open(path, "rb") as f:
        for chunk in iter(lambda: f.read(4096), b""):
            h.update(chunk)
    return h.hexdigest()


# --------------------------------------------------------
# OCR & Extraction
# --------------------------------------------------------


def azure_ocr(image_bytes: bytes) -> str:
    analyze_url = AZURE_ENDPOINT.rstrip("/") + \
        "/formrecognizer/documentModels/prebuilt-read:analyze?api-version=2023-07-31-preview"
    headers = {
        "Ocp-Apim-Subscription-Key": AZURE_KEY,
        "Content-Type": "application/octet-stream"
    }
    resp = requests.post(analyze_url, headers=headers, data=image_bytes)
    resp.raise_for_status()
    op_url = resp.headers["operation-location"]
    for _ in range(15):
        result = requests.get(op_url, headers={"Ocp-Apim-Subscription-Key": AZURE_KEY}).json()
        if result.get("status") == "succeeded":
            lines = []
            for page in result["analyzeResult"]["pages"]:
                for line in page["lines"]:
                    lines.append(line["content"])
            return "\n".join(lines)
        time.sleep(2)
    return ""


def tesseract_ocr(image_bytes: bytes) -> str:
    img = Image.open(io.BytesIO(image_bytes))
    return pytesseract.image_to_string(img)


def extract_text_from_image(image_bytes: bytes) -> str:
    text = ""
    try:
        text = azure_ocr(image_bytes)
    except Exception as e:
        logger.warning(f"Azure OCR failed: {e}")
    if not text.strip():
        try:
            text = tesseract_ocr(image_bytes)
        except Exception as e:
            logger.warning(f"Tesseract OCR failed: {e}")
    return text

### Answer
Yes, this is structurally correct now; you only need two very small clean‑ups.  

You already call st.set_page_config(...) once at the top of the file, so delete this part from inside main() to avoid the “set_page_config can only be called once” error:  
    # DELETE these lines (already done above)
    st.set_page_config(page_title="Respiratory AI Assistant", layout="wide")

Because you now render the chat as bubbles after each answer, the earlier block:
    # Show recent conversation
    if "chat_history" in st.session_state and st.session_state.chat_history:
        st.markdown("### 🧵 Conversation so far")
        for turn in st.session_state.chat_history[-8:]:
            role = "You" if turn["role"] == "user" else "Assistant"
            st.markdown(f"{role}: {turn['content']}")

is redundant; you can safely delete it to avoid showing the same conversation twice.

After those two deletions, your main() plus the new if query and search: block are in the right place and should run with the new pleasant theme and sequential chat bubbles.

def ensure_dir(path: str):
    os.makedirs(path, exist_ok=True)


def file_hash(path: str) -> str:
    h = hashlib.md5()
    with open(path, "rb") as f:
        for chunk in iter(lambda: f.read(4096), b""):
            h.update(chunk)
    return h.hexdigest()


# --------------------------------------------------------
# OCR & Extraction
# --------------------------------------------------------


def azure_ocr(image_bytes: bytes) -> str:
    analyze_url = AZURE_ENDPOINT.rstrip("/") + \
        "/formrecognizer/documentModels/prebuilt-read:analyze?api-version=2023-07-31-preview"
    headers = {
        "Ocp-Apim-Subscription-Key": AZURE_KEY,
        "Content-Type": "application/octet-stream"
    }
    resp = requests.post(analyze_url, headers=headers, data=image_bytes)
    resp.raise_for_status()
    op_url = resp.headers["operation-location"]
    for _ in range(15):
        result = requests.get(op_url, headers={"Ocp-Apim-Subscription-Key": AZURE_KEY}).json()
        if result.get("status") == "succeeded":
            lines = []
            for page in result["analyzeResult"]["pages"]:
                for line in page["lines"]:
                    lines.append(line["content"])
            return "\n".join(lines)
        time.sleep(2)
    return ""


def tesseract_ocr(image_bytes: bytes) -> str:
    img = Image.open(io.BytesIO(image_bytes))
    return pytesseract.image_to_string(img)


def extract_text_from_image(image_bytes: bytes) -> str:
    text = ""
    try:
        text = azure_ocr(image_bytes)
    except Exception as e:
        logger.warning(f"Azure OCR failed: {e}")
    if not text.strip():
        try:
            text = tesseract_ocr(image_bytes)
        except Exception as e:
            logger.warning(f"Tesseract OCR failed: {e}")
    return text

            model_kwargs={"device": "cpu"},

            search_type="mmr",
            search_kwargs={"k": 25, "fetch_k": 60, "lambda_mult": 0.4},
        )

                f"Doc {i} source={d.metadata.get('source')} "
                f"preview={d.page_content[:400].replace('\n', ' ')}"
            )

                "structure the answer into:\n"
                "1. Clinical presentation.\n"
                "2. Investigations (labs, imaging, other tests).\n"
                "3. Diagnosis and differential.\n"
                "4. Management and treatment (including specific medications, "
                "dose ranges, route, and duration when stated in the context).\n"
                "5. Follow‑up, monitoring, and red‑flags.\n\n"
                "Rules:\n"
                "- Respect the ongoing case: if the user asks a follow‑up question "
                "about 'this patient' or 'the previous CT', infer from the chat "
                "history what they refer to.\n"
                "- Every important factual statement must be supported by the "
                "knowledge base context.\n"
                "- Cite each major statement with its source file name "
                "(e.g. \"[source.pdf, pX]\").\n"
                "- If the context does NOT contain enough detail for a point, say so "
                "explicitly rather than guessing.\n"
                "- If the knowledge base overall does not answer the question, reply "
                "exactly: \"Insufficient data in provided materials.\" and nothing more.\n\n"
                "Latest user question:\n{question}\n\n"
                "Answer:\nAnswer without revealing your internal reasoning."
            ),
            input_variables=["chat_history", "kb_context", "question"],
        ).format(
            chat_history=chat_context_text,

## Turn 64
### Query
too bad can't see anything

### Answer
The text is almost invisible because the gradient background is too bright and the text itself is also light; calculators have light-blue cards on a very light background, so everything washes out visually.

Make the contrast higher by darkening text and slightly darkening the gradient. Replace your CUSTOM_CSS with this version (just copy‑paste over the old one):
CUSTOM_CSS = """
<style>
body {
    background-color: #0f172a;
}
[data-testid="stAppViewContainer"] {
    background: radial-gradient(circle at top, #111827 0%, #020617 45%, #020617 100%);
}
[data-testid="stHeader"] {
    background: rgba(0,0,0,0);
}
h1, h2, h3, h4, h5, h6, p, label, span, div {
    color: #e5e7eb !important;
}
.stTextArea textarea,
.stTextInput input {
    background-color: #020617 !important;
    color: #e5e7eb !important;
    border: 1px solid #4b5563 !important;
}
.stButton>button {
    background-color: #2563eb !important;
    color: white !important;
    border-radius: 999px !important;
    border: none !important;
}
.chat-container {
    padding: 1rem;
    background-color: #020617;
    border-radius: 16px;
    border: 1px solid #4b5563;
    margin-top: 1rem;
}
.chat-bubble-user {
    background-color: #1d4ed8;
    color: #e5e7eb;
    padding: 12px 16px;
    border-radius: 18px 18px 0 18px;
    margin-bottom: 8px;
}
.chat-bubble-assistant {
    background-color: #111827;
    color: #e5e7eb;
    padding: 12px 16px;
    border-radius: 18px 18px 18px 0;
    margin-bottom: 8px;
    border: 1px solid #4b5563;
}
.chat-meta {
    font-size: 0.75rem;
    color: #9ca3af;
    margin-bottom: 4px;
}
</style>

This gives you a dark background with light text and clearly visible chat bubbles and inputs, so everything should be readable even on a bright monitor.

## Turn 65
### Query
now how to continue chatting and make a discussion and follow up?

### Answer
You already have multi‑turn chat; you just need to keep typing follow‑up questions in the same text box and hit “Get Answer” each time. The code keeps history in st.session_state.chat_history and sends the last 6 turns plus KB context to the model on every new question, so it can understand “this patient”, “previous CT”, etc.

If you want the assistant to explicitly know it’s a follow‑up, phrase questions naturally, e.g.:
“What would you do if this patient is pregnant?”  
“How would management change if the CRP is rising despite antibiotics?”  

The new answer will be appended under “Recent conversation”, and both your previous question and the model’s earlier answer are passed back in chat_context_text each time, so the discussion flows as a continuous case rather than isolated queries.

---

## Turn 66
### Query
image.jpg

### Answer
That screen shows a PyTorch / sentence-transformers error: the model is on the meta device and cannot be moved with a normal .to() call.

In your file you already fixed this in build_db() by forcing CPU:  
embeddings = HuggingFaceEmbeddings(
    model_name=EMBED_MODEL,
    model_kwargs={"device": "cpu"}  # this avoids the meta-tensor issue
)
  

But inside main() you still create embeddings without model_kwargs in the “Test embedding model dimension” block. Change that block to match:  
embeddings = HuggingFaceEmbeddings(
    model_name=EMBED_MODEL,
    model_kwargs={"device": "cpu"}   # add this line
)
test_vec = embeddings.embed_query("test")
logger.info(f"✅ Embedding model: {EMBED_MODEL}, dimension: {len(test_vec)}")

Then, in the if query and search: block you already have the correct version:
embeddings = HuggingFaceEmbeddings(
    model_name=EMBED_MODEL,
    model_kwargs={"device": "cpu"},
)

After saving, rerun streamlit run main_resp_ai_The_Final_Version.py; the NotImplementedError should disappear and chat/follow‑ups will work.

---

                f"Doc {i} source={d.metadata.get('source')} "
                f"preview={d.page_content[:400].replace('\n', ' ')}"
            )


        # Limit total context length
        max_chars = 18000
        kb_context = ""
        for d in docs:
            if len(kb_context) + len(d.page_content) > max_chars:
                break
            kb_context += "\n\n" + d.page_content


        # 4) Build prompt with chat history + KB context
        prompt = PromptTemplate(
            template=(
                "You are an expert academic pulmonologist and intensivist.\n"
                "You are chatting with a clinician about a specific case.\n"
                "Use ONLY the information contained in the context AND prior turns of "
                "this chat. If an item is not supported by either, do not invent it.\n\n"
                "Conversation so far:\n{chat_history}\n\n"
                "Retrieved knowledge base context (guidelines, reviews, etc.):\n"
                "{kb_context}\n\n"
                "For the latest user question, if the information is available, "
                "structure the answer into:\n"
                "1. Clinical presentation.\n"
                "2. Investigations (labs, imaging, other tests).\n"
                "3. Diagnosis and differential.\n"
                "4. Management and treatment (including specific medications, "
                "dose ranges, route, and duration when stated in the context).\n"
                "5. Follow‑up, monitoring, and red‑flags.\n\n"
                "Rules:\n"
                "- Respect the ongoing case: if the user asks a follow‑up question "
                "about 'this patient' or 'the previous CT', infer from the chat "
                "history what they refer to.\n"
                "- Every important factual statement must be supported by the "
                "knowledge base context.\n"
                "- Cite each major statement with its source file name "
                "(e.g. \"[source.pdf, pX]\").\n"
                "- If the context does NOT contain enough detail for a point, say so "
                "explicitly rather than guessing.\n"
                "- If the knowledge base overall does not answer the question, reply "
                "exactly: \"Insufficient data in provided materials.\" and nothing more.\n\n"
                "Latest user question:\n{question}\n\n"
                "Answer:\nAnswer without revealing your internal reasoning."
            ),
            input_variables=["chat_history", "kb_context", "question"],
        ).format(
            chat_history=chat_context_text,
            kb_context=kb_context,
            question=query,
        )


        llm = Ollama(model=OLLAMA_MODEL, temperature=0.0, max_tokens=900)
        answer = llm.invoke(prompt)


        # 5) Save assistant answer into chat history
        st.session_state.chat_history.append({"role": "assistant", "content": answer})


        if "[" not in answer:
            st.warning("⚠️ Check sources—some statements may be unsourced.")


        # 6) Nice chat-style rendering (user + assistant bubbles)
        st.markdown("### 🗂️ Recent conversation")
        st.markdown('<div class="chat-container">', unsafe_allow_html=True)


        for msg in st.session_state.chat_history[-10:]:
            role_label = "🧑⚕️ You" if msg["role"] == "user" else "🤖 Assistant"
            bubble_class = "chat-bubble-user" if msg["role"] == "user" else "chat-bubble-assistant"


            st.markdown(
                f"""
                <div class="chat-meta">{role_label}</div>
                <div class="{bubble_class}">{msg["content"]}</div>
                """,
                unsafe_allow_html=True,
            )


        st.markdown("</div>", unsafe_allow_html=True)


        # 7) Sources section under the chat
        st.markdown(
            '<div style="background:#f1f3f4;padding:1rem;border-radius:5px;margin-top:1rem;">',
            unsafe_allow_html=True,
        )
        st.markdown("### 📚 Sources")
        for d in docs:
            st.markdown(f"- {d.metadata['source']}")
        st.markdown("</div>", unsafe_allow_html=True)


    calculator_section()

    main()

def build_db(rebuild: bool = False, progress_callback=None) -> List[str]:
    ensure_dir(DB_DIR)
    processed = {}
    if os.path.exists(PROCESSED_TRACK) and not rebuild:
        with open(PROCESSED_TRACK, "r") as f:
            processed = json.load(f)
    if rebuild:
        shutil.rmtree(DB_DIR)
        ensure_dir(DB_DIR)
        processed = {}


    pdfs = [f for f in os.listdir(PDF_DIR) if f.lower().endswith(".pdf")]
    total_pdfs = len(pdfs)
    start_time = time.time()


    warnings = []
    docs = []


    for i, fname in enumerate(pdfs, 1):
        path = os.path.join(PDF_DIR, fname)


        h = file_hash(path)
        if processed.get(fname) == h:
            if progress_callback:
                percent_done = i / total_pdfs * 100
                progress_callback(fname, percent_done, 0)
            continue


        text, w = extract_text_from_pdf(path)
        for msg in w:
            warnings.append(f"{fname}: {msg}")
        if text.strip():
            docs.append(Document(page_content=text, metadata={"source": fname}))
        else:
            warnings.append(f"{fname}: empty document")


        processed[fname] = h


        if progress_callback:
            percent_done = i / total_pdfs * 100
            elapsed = time.time() - start_time
            remaining = (elapsed / i) * (total_pdfs - i) if i > 0 else 0
            progress_callback(fname, percent_done, remaining)


    with open(PROCESSED_TRACK, "w") as f:
        json.dump(processed, f)


    splitter = RecursiveCharacterTextSplitter(chunk_size=1000, chunk_overlap=200)
    raw_chunks = splitter.split_documents(docs)
    chunks = [c for c in raw_chunks if c.page_content.strip()]


    if not chunks:
        return warnings + ["No chunks to index"]


    embeddings = HuggingFaceEmbeddings(
    model_name=EMBED_MODEL,
    model_kwargs={"device": "cpu"}  # force CPU, avoids meta-tensor device issue
    )


    if os.listdir(DB_DIR):
        store = Chroma(persist_directory=DB_DIR, embedding_function=embeddings)
        store.add_documents(chunks)
    else:
        Chroma.from_documents(chunks, embedding=embeddings, persist_directory=DB_DIR)


    return warnings

        model_name=EMBED_MODEL,
        model_kwargs={"device": "cpu"}
    )
    test_vec = embeddings.embed_query("test")

Keep the other two embeddings blocks:
Inside build_db(...) (with model_kwargs={"device": "cpu"})  
Inside if query and search: (with model_kwargs={"device": "cpu"})

## Turn 71
### Query
how to run build_new_db.py_V2.py

### Answer
From your project root (D:\Dev\Active\RespAI_Project), run it like any normal Python script in the same virtual env you use for Streamlit:
cd D:\Dev\Active\RespAI_Project
.\venv\Scripts\Activate.ps1

python build_new_db.py_V2.py

or, if python points elsewhere, use:
py build_new_db.py_V2.py

The script will execute once, build/update your Chroma DB, then exit; after that you just run the Streamlit app as usual with:
streamlit run main_resp_ai_The_Final_Version.py

## Turn 72
### Query
where chroma will be installed ? and if not found will it be contain all the pdfs or what?

### Answer
In your project, Chroma’s files are stored in the folder you set as DB_DIR, i.e.:
DB_DIR = os.path.join(BASE_DIR, "chroma_db")

BASE_DIR is the directory of main_resp_ai_The_Final_Version.py, so Chroma will persist into:
D:\Dev\Active\RespAI_Project\chroma_db


What it contains:
It does not contain the original PDFs.  
It stores the vector index: embeddings, metadata, and an internal SQLite / DuckDB structure used for fast retrieval.
Your PDFs remain in the pdfs folder:
PDF_DIR = os.path.join(BASE_DIR, "pdfs")
so you should keep both pdfs (raw data) and chroma_db (indexed data).

If chroma_db does not exist or is empty, your app shows the “Database missing” error and you must run either build_db() (via sidebar buttons) or python build_new_db.py_V2.py to scan all PDFs in pdfs, embed them, and create the Chroma index.

---

## Turn 73
### Query
i want to build a new fresh chroma_db

### Answer
To build a completely fresh chroma_db, you have two options; both do the same thing in your code.
1. Make sure your PDFs are in D:\Dev\Active\RespAI_Project\pdfs.
2. Run the app:

   powershell
   cd D:\Dev\Active\RespAI_Project
   .\venv\Scripts\Activate.ps1
   streamlit run main_resp_ai_The_Final_Version.py
   
3. In the sidebar, click “🔄 Rebuild Database”.  
This calls build_db(rebuild=True, ...), deletes chroma_db, and rebuilds it from all PDFs.
If build_new_db.py_V2.py is wired to use build_db(rebuild=True) (as we discussed):
cd D:\Dev\Active\RespAI_Project
.\venv\Scripts\Activate.ps1
python build_new_db.py_V2.py

That will also delete the existing chroma_db folder and recreate it with fresh embeddings for all PDFs in pdfs.

---

## Turn 74
### Query
i want a new fresh on in a different folder so the old one not deleted and i get a new different one what to change inside the code?

### Answer
You can keep the old chroma_db and build a brand‑new one in a different folder by changing the DB_DIR path (and, if you want, only in the script that builds the new DB).

For example:
NEW_DB_DIR = os.path.join(BASE_DIR, "chroma_db_v2")

If you want the app to use this new DB permanently, edit DB_DIR at the top of your main file:
DB_DIR = os.path.join(BASE_DIR, "chroma_db_v2")

This will leave the old chroma_db folder untouched and make everything (build_db, Streamlit app) read/write chroma_db_v2 instead.
In build_new_db.py_V2.py, set:
DB_DIR = os.path.join(BASE_DIR, "chroma_db_v2")
In main_resp_ai_The_Final_Version.py you can keep DB_DIR pointing to the old or new directory depending on which DB you want the app to query.

After changing the path, run the builder (sidebar “Rebuild Database” or python build_new_db.py_V2.py). A new folder chroma_db_v2 will appear alongside the old chroma_db, and it will contain a separate index for the same or different PDFs, depending on what’s in your pdfs folder at build time.

#!/usr/bin/env python3
"""
PDF → BAAI/bge-large-en (1024-dim) → Chroma DB Builder
- Real-time console feedback
- Resumable on two levels:
    1) PDF text extraction (processed_files.json)
    2) Chroma indexing (indexed_files.json)
- Safe after laptop crash / power loss:
    - Already extracted PDFs are skipped
    - Only PDFs not yet indexed are (re)added to Chroma
"""


import os
import json
import logging
import time
from pathlib import Path
from typing import List, Tuple
import sys
import io
import hashlib


# Optional progress bar (not required)
try:
    from tqdm import tqdm  # noqa: F401
    TQDM_AVAILABLE = True
except ImportError:
    TQDM_AVAILABLE = False
    print("⚠️  tqdm not installed - install with: pip install tqdm")


import fitz  # PyMuPDF
from PyPDF2 import PdfReader
from PIL import Image
import pytesseract
import requests


from langchain_huggingface import HuggingFaceEmbeddings
from langchain_chroma import Chroma
from langchain_core.documents import Document
from langchain_text_splitters import RecursiveCharacterTextSplitter



# ----------------------------------------------------
# CONFIG
# ----------------------------------------------------
logging.basicConfig(level=logging.INFO, format="%(asctime)s %(levelname)s %(message)s")
logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)


BASE_DIR = Path(__file__).resolve().parent


PDF_INPUT_DIR = BASE_DIR / "pdfs"
DB_DIR = os.path.join(BASE_DIR, "chroma_db_v2")
PROCESSED_TRACK = BASE_DIR / "processed_files.json"  # text extracted
INDEXED_TRACK = BASE_DIR / "indexed_files.json"      # chunks added to Chroma


EMBED_MODEL = "BAAI/bge-large-en"  # 1024-dim
CHUNK_SIZE = 1200
CHUNK_OVERLAP = 300


# Tesseract path
pytesseract.pytesseract.tesseract_cmd = r"C:\Program Files\Tesseract-OCR\tesseract.exe"


# Azure OCR (optional)
AZURE_ENDPOINT = "https://respai-rg.cognitiveservices.azure.com/"
AZURE_KEY = os.getenv("AZURE_KEY")



print("🚀" * 40)
print("📚 Resumable Medical PDF → BAAI/bge-large-en → Chroma DB Builder")
print("🚀" * 40)
print(f"📁 Input PDFs:   {PDF_INPUT_DIR}")
print(f"💾 Output DB:    {NEW_DB_DIR}")
print(f"🧠 Embed model:  {EMBED_MODEL} (1024-dim)")

# ----------------------------------------------------
# Utility: pretty status lines
# ----------------------------------------------------
def print_status(stage: str, detail: str = "", extra: str = ""):
    """
    Print a single-line status with stage + detail.
    Example:
      [EXTRACT] pleural_guideline.pdf | 3/100
    """
    sys.stdout.write("\r" + " " * 140)
    msg = f"[{stage}] {detail}"
    if extra:
        msg += f" | {extra}"
    sys.stdout.write("\r" + msg)
    sys.stdout.flush()



def print_banner(msg: str):
    print("\n" + "=" * 80)
    print(f"✅ {msg}")
    print("=" * 80 + "\n")



# ----------------------------------------------------
# OCR helpers
# ----------------------------------------------------
def azure_ocr_fallback(image_bytes: bytes) -> str:
    """Try Azure OCR, return text or empty string."""
    if not AZURE_KEY:
        return ""
    try:
        analyze_url = (
            AZURE_ENDPOINT.rstrip("/")
            + "/formrecognizer/documentModels/prebuilt-read:analyze"
            + "?api-version=2023-07-31-preview"
        )
        headers = {
            "Ocp-Apim-Subscription-Key": AZURE_KEY,
            "Content-Type": "application/octet-stream",
        }
        resp = requests.post(analyze_url, headers=headers, data=image_bytes, timeout=30)
        resp.raise_for_status()
        op_url = resp.headers["operation-location"]


        for _ in range(20):
            result = requests.get(
                op_url,
                headers={"Ocp-Apim-Subscription-Key": AZURE_KEY},
                timeout=30,
            ).json()
            if result.get("status") == "succeeded":
                lines = []
                for page in result["analyzeResult"]["pages"]:
                    for line in page["lines"]:
                        lines.append(line["content"])
                return "\n".join(lines)
            time.sleep(1.5)
    except Exception as e:
        logger.debug(f"Azure OCR failed: {e}")
    return ""

# Text extraction for medical PDFs
# ----------------------------------------------------

        src = doc.metadata.get("source")
        if not indexed.get(src):
            docs_to_index.append(doc)


    # (b) Any previously extracted docs (processed=True) but not yet indexed
    for filename, done in processed.items():
        if not done:
            continue
        if indexed.get(filename):
            continue  # already fully indexed


        # Load text again from PDF (one more time, but only for not-indexed)
        pdf_path = PDF_INPUT_DIR / filename
        if not pdf_path.exists():
            continue


        print_status("RELOAD", filename, "for missing index")
        text, warnings, method = extract_medical_pdf(pdf_path)
        all_warnings.extend([f"{filename}: {w}" for w in warnings])
        if text.strip():
            doc = Document(
                page_content=text.strip(),
                metadata={"source": filename, "method": method, "chars": len(text)},
            )
            docs_to_index.append(doc)


    # Deduplicate docs_to_index by source (just in case)
    by_source = {}
    for doc in docs_to_index:
        src = doc.metadata.get("source")
        by_source[src] = doc
    docs_to_index = list(by_source.values())


    if not docs_to_index:
        print_banner("No documents pending indexing into Chroma. All up-to-date.")
        if all_warnings:
            print("⚠️ Warnings:")
            for w in all_warnings[:15]:
                print("   •", w)
            if len(all_warnings) > 15:
                print(f"   • ... and {len(all_warnings) - 15} more")
        return


    print_banner(f"{len(docs_to_index)} documents will be indexed into Chroma this run")


    # ---------------------------
    # 3) Chunking docs to index
    # ---------------------------
    print_status("CHUNK", f"{len(docs_to_index)} docs → chunks")
    splitter = RecursiveCharacterTextSplitter(
        chunk_size=CHUNK_SIZE,
        chunk_overlap=CHUNK_OVERLAP,
        separators=["\n\n", "\n", ". ", " ", ""],
        keep_separator=True,
    )
    chunks_to_add = splitter.split_documents(docs_to_index)
    print_banner(
        f"Chunking complete: {len(chunks_to_add)} chunks from {len(docs_to_index)} docs"
    )


    if not chunks_to_add:
        print("ℹ️ No chunks produced for indexing. Exiting.")
        return


    # ---------------------------
    # 4) Embeddings & Chroma
    # ---------------------------
    print_status("EMBED", "Loading BAAI/bge-large-en...")
    embeddings = HuggingFaceEmbeddings(model_name=EMBED_MODEL)
    test_vec = embeddings.embed_query("test")
    print_banner(f"Embedding model ready; dim = {len(test_vec)}")


    print_status("CHROMA", "Updating vector database...")
    if any(NEW_DB_DIR.iterdir()):
        # DB exists → open & append
        vectorstore = Chroma(
            persist_directory=str(NEW_DB_DIR),
            embedding_function=embeddings,
        )
        vectorstore.add_documents(chunks_to_add)
    else:
        # First run → build from scratch
        vectorstore = Chroma.from_documents(
            documents=chunks_to_add,
            embedding=embeddings,
            persist_directory=str(NEW_DB_DIR),
        )
    #vectorstore.persist()
    print_banner("Chroma update complete")


    # ---------------------------
    # 5) Mark docs as indexed
    # ---------------------------
    for doc in docs_to_index:
        src = doc.metadata.get("source")
        indexed[src] = True


    with open(INDEXED_TRACK, "w", encoding="utf-8") as f:
        json.dump(indexed, f, indent=2)


    print_banner("🎉 DATABASE UPDATED SUCCESSFULLY (RESUMABLE INDEXING)")
    print("📊 This run:")
    print(f"   • Docs indexed:        {len(docs_to_index)}")
    print(f"   • Chunks added:        {len(chunks_to_add)}")
    print(f"   • DB location:         {NEW_DB_DIR.absolute()}")


    if all_warnings:
        print(f"\n⚠️ Warnings this run ({len(all_warnings)}):")
        for w in all_warnings[:15]:
            print("   •", w)
        if len(all_warnings) > 15:
            print(f"   • ... and {len(all_warnings) - 15} more")



# ----------------------------------------------------
# Entry point
# ----------------------------------------------------
if __name__ == "__main__":
    start = time.time()
    try:
        print("⏱️ Starting resumable build / update...")
        build_new_db()
        elapsed = time.time() - start
        print(f"\n⏱️ Total time this run: {elapsed/60:.1f} minutes")
        print("ℹ️ Already processed/indexed PDFs will be skipped on next run.")
    except KeyboardInterrupt:
        print("\n⛔ Stopped by user (Ctrl+C)")
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"\n💥 UNEXPECTED ERROR: {e}")
        import traceback


        traceback.print_exc()
        print("\n🔧 Fix the error and re-run; progress files will resume work.")

### Answer
Two small fixes:

1. Define NEW_DB_DIR at the top (you already use it later but only defined DB_DIR).  
2. Force the embeddings in this script to CPU, like in your main app.

Here is the minimal patch.

At the top, under BASE_DIR = Path(file).resolve().parent, replace your DB lines with:
PDF_INPUT_DIR = BASE_DIR / "pdfs"
DB_DIR = BASE_DIR / "chroma_db"
NEW_DB_DIR = BASE_DIR / "chroma_db_v2"

PROCESSED_TRACK = BASE_DIR / "processed_files.json"  # text extracted
INDEXED_TRACK = BASE_DIR / "indexed_files.json"      # chunks added to Chroma

and in the header prints:
print(f"📁 Input PDFs:   {PDF_INPUT_DIR}")
print(f"💾 Output DB:    {NEW_DB_DIR}")
print(f"🧠 Embed model:  {EMBED_MODEL} (1024-dim)")

In the “EMBED & Chroma” section, change:
embeddings = HuggingFaceEmbeddings(model_name=EMBED_MODEL)

to:
embeddings = HuggingFaceEmbeddings(
    model_name=EMBED_MODEL,
    model_kwargs={"device": "cpu"},
)

After these edits:
cd D:\Dev\Active\RespAI_Project
.\venv\Scripts\Activate.ps1
python build_new_db.py_V2.py

This will build a new, resumable Chroma DB in D:\Dev\Active\RespAI_Project\chroma_db_v2 without touching your old chroma_db.

## Turn 76
### Query
⏱️ Starting resumable build / update...

================================================================================
✅ Found 87 PDFs (resumable, incremental mode)
================================================================================

                                                                                                                        [SKIP] 2022_PH_Guidelines_Essential_messages.pdf | Already e                                                                                                                        [SKIP] A CLINICAL GUIDE TO OCCUPATIONAL AND ENVIRONMENTAL LUNG DISEASES (2012) (Z-Library).pdf | Already extracted (2/87                                                                                                                        [SKIP] Acute Exacerbations of Pulmonary Diseases (Pierre-Régis Burgel, Marco Contoli etc.) (Z-Library).pdf | Already ext
what does skip here mean?

### Answer
“SKIP” here is expected and good.

It means:
That PDF’s text was already extracted in a previous run, and it is marked in processed_files.json as done.
The script does not re‑run OCR or text extraction for it now, which saves a lot of time and lets the process be resumable after crashes or interruptions.

If a file has never been processed before, you’ll see “EXTRACT / EXTRACT✓ / OCR” messages instead of “SKIP”, and only those new or not‑yet‑indexed PDFs will be re‑embedded and added to the new Chroma DB.

## Turn 77
### Query
but i want to rebuild a new chroma db including all the pdfs so it has to extract all files from scratch do i need to change some pieces of the code and/or folder position?

### Answer
To force a truly fresh Chroma DB (all PDFs re‑extracted and re‑embedded), you need to reset the tracking files and the DB folder, not change the code.

From PowerShell (venv can be on or off):
cd D:\Dev\Active\RespAI_Project
del processed_files.json
del indexed_files.json
rmdir /S /Q chroma_db_v2   # or chroma_db if that is the one you use


Now the script will think nothing was processed or indexed before.
.\venv\Scripts\Activate.ps1
python build_new_db.py_V2.py

This time you should not see [SKIP] lines; every PDF will go through EXTRACT and then be indexed into the new chroma_db_v2.

No code changes are required as long as:
NEW_DB_DIR = BASE_DIR / "chroma_db_v2"
PDF_INPUT_DIR = BASE_DIR / "pdfs"

are set correctly in build_new_db.py_V2.py, and your main app’s DB_DIR points to the DB you want to use.

## Turn 78
### Query
and is this going to change the already founf chroma in the previous work found in D:\Dev\Active\RespAI_Project\chroma_db

### Answer
No, as long as you keep using the v2 folder, the old DB at D:\Dev\Active\RespAI_Project\chroma_db is untouched.
build_new_db.py_V2.py is configured to write to chroma_db_v2 (via NEW_DB_DIR).  
When you delete processed_files.json, indexed_files.json, and chroma_db_v2, you are only resetting the new DB and its progress, not chroma_db.  
The original chroma_db will remain on disk until you explicitly delete it.

If you want the Streamlit app to use the new DB, set:
DB_DIR = os.path.join(BASE_DIR, "chroma_db_v2")

in main_resp_ai_The_Final_Version.py; otherwise it will keep using the old chroma_db.

### Answer
The errors are just PowerShell syntax issues; nothing dangerous happened.

processed_files.json and indexed_files.json simply don’t exist yet, so PowerShell complains when you try to delete them. That’s fine; there’s nothing to reset there.

In PowerShell, use Remove-Item with parameters, not rmdir /S /Q (that’s CMD syntax).

From D:\Dev\Active\RespAI_Project:
Remove-Item -Recurse -Force .\chroma_db_v2

If you instead want to delete the old DB:
Remove-Item -Recurse -Force .\chroma_db

After that, run the builder again:
.\venv\Scripts\Activate.ps1
python build_new_db.py_V2.py

This will create a completely fresh Chroma DB in whichever folder your script points to (NEW_DB_DIR).

## Turn 81
### Query
now let's install some 3rd party apps on the destroyer 05 2025 byd infotainment screen

### Answer
On 2025‑plus BYD systems (including Destroyer 05), you can usually sideload Android APKs, but the exact steps depend on software version and region; some firmwares block this unless you first “unlock” the installer.
Newer 2024–2025 builds (e.g. 2310, 2503) often block third‑party installs by default; some require a downgrade + unlock, then re‑update.
Any modification may affect warranty or future OTA updates; do this only if you accept that risk and are comfortable recovering firmware.

Many BYD head units accept APKs from a USB when placed in a special folder:

1. Format a USB drive to FAT32.
2. On the USB, create a folder named exactly (examples seen in the wild):  
third party apps  
Third party apps+<country code> (some guides mention adding country code, e.g. Third party apps+US).
3. Copy the APK files you want into that folder (Spotify “car” builds, YouTube, Waze, Froid/FDroid, etc.).
4. Plug the USB into the infotainment port (often port 2 inside the armrest).
5. When prompted for a code, common codes for BYD multimedia are:  
20211231 for pre‑1.5  
BYD6125F or GHY0613byd for later systems (varies by firmware).
6. If accepted, you’ll see a file browser or installer; select each APK and install.

If your Destroyer 05 accepts this without errors, you’re done; this is the cleanest method.

On 2024–2025 firmwares, you may get a blocker popup. Two common approaches exist:

Used on Seal/Atto/M6 and reported to work on other 2024+ models:
Enable developer / debug mode on the head unit (there is usually a hidden menu reachable via tapping software version repeatedly, then entering a code; exact path can differ).
Connect the BYD infotainment to the same Wi‑Fi network as your phone.
Use a phone tool that talks ADB over network:  
Android: Easy Fire Tools.  
iOS: atvTools (paid).
From the tool, push and install a special PackageInstallerUnlocked.apk (or similar) that disables the third‑party block.
After that, normal APK installs no longer show the blocker popup and work “as per normal.”

This is more advanced but avoids firmware flashing.

If your software is on a locked version where USB/ADB tricks fail (e.g. some 2310+ builds), community tutorials describe:

1. Download an older multimedia firmware (e.g. 2307) that still allows APK installs.
2. Put its BYDUpdatePackage folder on a FAT32 USB root as instructed.
3. Plug into the car and perform the downgrade from the update menu.
4. Install PackageInstallerUnlocked.apk from the same USB to permanently unlock the installer.
5. Then update again to the latest version (2310/2310220 etc.); the unlock persists across updates.

This is powerful but also the riskiest (firmware flashing). Only attempt if you’ve read the full guide for your exact version and are comfortable recovering from a failed update.

Given you’re technical and willing to experiment:
First try the USB “third party apps” folder + code route; it’s simple and reversible.
If blocked, see whether your software version matches the ADB sideloading guides (check YouTube “BYD M6 sideloading 2025” and “USB method” videos; these show the exact menu paths and codes).
Only consider downgrade/unlock if both above fail and you’ve confirmed from BYD communities (BYD Discord / Reddit / FB groups) that your exact firmware build and region are supported.

If you tell me your Destroyer 05’s multimedia version string (e.g. 13.1.32.2310…) and region, I can suggest the most likely working method and what tools/APKs to start with.

## Turn 82
### Query
how to find Destroyer 05’s multimedia version string

### Answer
On BYD cars (including Destroyer 05), the multimedia/system version is shown in the Settings → System → Version area of the main screen.

Here is the usual path:

1. Turn the car on so the big central screen is active.  
2. Tap the gear icon or “Settings” on the home screen.
3. In Settings, open the “System” section (sometimes called “System settings”).
4. Look for an item like “Version”, “Software”, or “System version”, then tap “Version details” / “Software detail”.

On that screen you should see a long string like:
13.1.22.23240301.1 (example)  

The first line is the software version (this is what we need for sideload guides), and a second line often shows firmware version.

If the menus differ on the Destroyer 05, send a photo of your Settings screen and I can map the exact taps.

### Answer
On this screen you’re in Settings → DLink → Application management, which is the app manager, not the version page.   

To see the system version string on this style of BYD UI, try:

1. Tap the “Version management” tab at the top (just left of “Application management”).  
2. In the left column, look for something like “System update”, “Local update”, or “Version information” and tap it.   
3. On the resulting page, there is usually a line with a long version string (numbers and dots). That’s the multimedia/software version we need.   

If “Version management” doesn’t show it, back out to the main Settings categories (the left vertical menu) and look for an entry like “Vehicle Settings → System info” or “System → About”; the version page is typically under those.

## Turn 86
### Query
let's start with USB “third party apps”

### Answer
Your system version 13.1.22.2403046.1 is in the group where the USB “third party apps” sideload usually works, though some regions still block it.   

1. On your PC, insert a USB stick (8–32 GB is fine).  
2. Format it as FAT32 (Quick format is OK).   
3. On the empty USB, create a folder named exactly:  

   text
   third party apps
     

   Use all lower‑case with spaces, no quotes. This name is what the BYD multimedia system scans for. 

4. Download a couple of test APKs (phone browser is fine): for example a simple file manager or browser APK (not bundles, plain .apk). Copy them into the third party apps folder.   

1. Start the car and wait for the infotainment to boot.  
2. Plug the USB into the data USB port (often the inner port in the front armrest or under the screen; same one used for Android Auto/CarPlay).   
3. After a few seconds, a popup should appear about updating or installing apps. If nothing shows, go to:  
DLink → Application management and look for something like “USB install” or “Install package”.   

On many 13.x builds, when the system detects third party apps, it asks for a code before showing the APK list. Community‑reported codes include:   

Try in this order if a numeric/alphanumeric keypad appears:

1. 20211231  
2. BYD6125F  
3. GHY0613byd  

If one is accepted, you should see a file browser listing your APKs in third party apps; tap each APK to install. 
Installed apps usually appear under DLink → App or on the main launcher grid.   
You may need to grant permissions the first time you run them (Storage, Location, etc.).   

Different reactions are possible on your build: 
No popup at all, no installer UI:  
Confirm the folder name is third party apps (no extra spaces or extension).  
Try another USB stick and ensure it’s FAT32, not exFAT/NTFS. 
Popup appears but installing is blocked / error about permissions:  
That means your firmware has the “third‑party ban” enabled. In that case the next step is the ADB sideload/unlock method using a phone tool (Easy Fire Tools / atvTools) to push an unlocked installer, which we can walk through next. 

Try the USB method once and tell me exactly what you see (popup text, any code request, or error); then we’ll adjust the next step based on your screen.

## Turn 87
### Query
should the files be in apk format or xapk fine?

### Answer
Use plain .apk files only, not .xapk or .apkm.

The BYD installer (both USB and ADB methods) expects standard APK packages and cannot handle XAPK split‑APK bundles, so installs with .xapk usually fail or are not detected at all.

---
